$(document).ready(function(){ 
		$("#waiting").show();

    var url=window.location.href;
    if(url.match(/MemberNo/g))
    {
		var urlSplit=url.split("=");
		var firststring=urlSplit[0];
		var secondstring=urlSplit[1];
		var splitfirst=firststring.split("?")
		var promocode=splitfirst[1];
		//alert(promocode);
		var splitsecond="";
		if(secondstring!=undefined){splitsecond=secondstring.split("&");}
		var membership=splitsecond[1]





       var pageName='http://stg.qatarairways.com/iw-cc/qmiles/OfferRegistration.jsp';		
		var MemberNo =urlSplit[2];
		var promoCode =splitsecond[0];
		//alert("MemberNo : "+MemberNo);
		//alert("promoCode : "+promoCode);

		//console.log("MemberNo : "+MemberNo);
		//console.log("promoCode : "+promoCode);		
		$(".prmoCode").text(promoCode+". ");
	
	   //alert("session there");
		$.ajax({
			type: "GET",
			url: pageName,
            data: ({ffpNumber : MemberNo,promoCode:promoCode}),			
			cache: false,
			dataType: "html",
			success: function(content){
            //alert(content);
				//document.getElementById("pcoffersregtemp").innerHTML="";
				//document.getElementById("pcoffersregtemp").innerHTML=content; 
				//alert(content);
				
				var responseval = document.getElementById("offer_reg_result").innerHTML;
				//alert("responseval--"+responseval);
				if(responseval.indexOf("true")!= -1){					
					window.location.href = "http://stg.qatarairways.com/content/global/en/Privilege-Club/offer-registration-confirmation.html";
				}
				else if(responseval.indexOf("Promo code is null or empty.")!= -1){
				window.location.href="http://stg.qatarairways.com/content/global/en/Privilege-Club/offer-registration-failed.html"
					//alert("Internal Service Error, Please try again later");
					//$(".reg_stats").css("display","block");
					//$(".reg_msg_empty_PC").css("display","block");
					//$("#waiting").hide();
				}else if(responseval.indexOf("false")!= -1){	
					window.location.href="http://stg.qatarairways.com/content/global/en/Privilege-Club/offer-registration-failed.html"
					//$(".reg_stats").css("display","block");
					//$(".reg_msg_empty_PC").css("display","block");
					//$("#waiting").hide();
				}else{	
					$(".reg_stats").css("display","block");
					$(".reg_msg_empty_PC").css("display","block");
					$("#waiting").hide();
				}			
			},
			error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError){	
           // alert(content);
				//alert("Error");
		    }

		});
	  
    }
	
	});
	

	
	function offercancel(){ 
		window.location.href = 'cancel';
	}
	
	function cpmAutoLogin(){  
		var userid=$("#PostQmilesUsrName").val();
		var pwd=$("#PostQmilesPwd").val();
        var encryptpwdjsp='http://stg.qatarairways.com/iw-cc/qatar/cpm_encryption.jsp';
		if(userid=='' || pwd==''){
			alert('enter valid credentials');
			return false;
		} 
		var cpmloginobj = getFieldByID("QmilesOfferReg");
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: encryptpwdjsp,
			data: ({passwordval : pwd}),						
			cache: false,
			dataType: "html",
			success: function(content)
			{
				document.getElementById("pcoffersregtemp").innerHTML="";
				document.getElementById("pcoffersregtemp").innerHTML=content;
				var encyrptpwd = document.getElementById("jspresult").innerHTML;
				$('#PostQmilesPwd').val(encyrptpwd);
				cpmloginobj.action = "https://cpm.qatarairways.com/cpm/views/verfiyUserQrHome.xhtml";
				cpmloginobj.submit();
			},
			error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError){	
			 
			}			
		});
		
	}
	$(document).ajaxComplete(function () {
		var memNameAfterAllAjax=$("#totalUserInfo .memberNam").text();
		if(memNameAfterAllAjax!=''){
			$(".userName").text(" "+memNameAfterAllAjax);
		}
	});

		var tabpanid= $(this).attr("aria-controls"); //find out what tab panel this tab controls  
        var tabpan = $("#"+tabpanid);  
        $(".language-tabs-accordion li[role='tabpanel']").attr("aria-hidden","true").addClass('fade').removeClass('active in'); //hide all the panels 
        tabpan.attr("aria-hidden","false").addClass('active in').removeClass('fade');  // show our panel
 	});

                   <!-- drop-block-title -->
                   <strong class="drop-block-title" tabindex="0">Offers</strong> 
                   <span class="forward drop-title"></span> 
                   <!-- drop-block-offers --> 
                   <div></div> 
                   <input type="hidden" id="vertical-block2-seletion" value="dynamicTeaser"> 
                   <div id="vertical-block2-verticalDynamicTeaser"> 
                    <input type="hidden" id="vertical-block2-horizontal-3" value="205.153"> 
                    <input type="hidden" id="vertical-block2-origin" value="bom"> 
                    <input id="vertical-block2-destinationRepo" type="hidden" value="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/destinations/repository"> 
                    <!-- drop-block-offers --> 
                    <div class="hidden vertical-block2-inputIataCodes">
                     ATL
                    </div> 
                    <div class="drop-block-offers teaser-ATL"> 
                     <!-- drop-block-offers-promo --> 
                     <div class="drop-block-offers-promo"> 
                      <a target="_blank"> 
                       <div class="imagery"></div> 
                       <div class="drop-block-offers-text"> 
                        <strong class="drop-block-offers-title"></strong> 
                        <span class="drop-block-offers-price"></span>

                    <!-- drop-block-more-link --> 
                    <div class="drop-block-more-link"> 
                     <a class="btn-more pull-right" href="/content/in/en/offers.html" target="_self">More fares <span class="icon icon-arrow-right2 icon-rotate-rtl"></span> </a>

                      <a target="_blank"> 
                       <div class="imagery"></div>

                        <strong class="drop-block-offers-title"></strong> 
                        <span class="drop-block-offers-price"></span>

                    <!-- drop-block-offers end --> 
                    <!-- drop-block-more-link --> 
                    <div class="drop-block-more-link"> 
                     <a class="btn-more pull-right" href="/content/in/en/offers.html" target="_self">More fares <span class="icon icon-arrow-right2 icon-rotate-rtl"></span> </a> 
                    </div> 
                    <!-- drop-block-more-link end --> 
                   </div> 
                   <script>
	$(document).ready(function() {
		try{
			var node = "vertical-block2";
			var seletion = $('#' + node + '-seletion').val();
			/*var origin = getCookieValue("fromIata");
			if (origin == undefined || origin == null || origin == '') {
				origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val();
			}
			*/
			var origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val();
			var pricingResponse = $getHPricingData(origin);
			var destinationIataCodes = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + node + '-inputIataCodes');
			if (seletion == 'dynamicTeaser') {
				$(destinationIataCodes).each(function() {
					var destination = $(this).text();
					var teaserNode = "teaser-" + destination;
					$getPricingDataVTeaser(node, teaserNode, pricingResponse, destination);
					$getDestinationRepoResultVTeaser(node, teaserNode, destination);
				});
			}
		} catch(err) {} 
	});

	var $getHPricingData = function(origin) {
		var pricingResponse;
		if(origin != undefined && origin != null && origin != "") {
            origin = origin.toUpperCase();
            origin = origin.trim();
			getPricingResponse(origin, function(data) {
				//console.log('getPricingResponse:' + data);
				pricingResponse = data;
			});
		}
		return pricingResponse;
	}
	
	var $getPricingDataVTeaser = function(node, teaserNode, pricingResponse, destination) {

		if(destination != undefined && destination != null && destination != "") {
            destination = destination.toUpperCase();
            destination = destination.trim();
        }

		 //console.log("pricingResponse::::::::::::" + pricingResponse);
		if(pricingResponse != undefined && pricingResponse != null && pricingResponse != "" && pricingResponse.length != 0) {
			var offerResponseArray = pricingResponse.offerResponseList;
			if (offerResponseArray.length != 0) {
				var currencyCode = offerResponseArray[0].currencyCode;
				var destinationFaresArray = offerResponseArray[0].destinationFares;
				if (destinationFaresArray.length != 0) {
					var destData = getDestinationPricingData(destinationFaresArray, destination);
					if (destData.length != 0) {
						$.each(destData[0].lowestFares, function(key, value) {
							if (value.cabinClass == 'ECONOMY') {
								$('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.drop-block-offers-price').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
								$('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('a').attr('href',value.deepLink);

							}
						});
					}
				}
			}
		}
					
	}

	var $getDestinationRepoResultVTeaser = function(node, teaserNode, destination) {
		if(destination != undefined && destination != null && destination != "") {
            destination = destination.toUpperCase();
            destination = destination.trim();
        }
		var destinationRepoPath = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('#' + node + '-destinationRepo').val();
		var destnRepoResult;
		getDestinationRepoData(destination,destinationRepoPath, function(data) {
			//console.log('getPricingResponse:' + data);
			destnRepoResult = data;
		});
		if (destnRepoResult != '' && destnRepoResult != undefined && destnRepoResult != null) {
			var imagePath = destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3;
			var imageData,imageExtension;
			if(imagePath != undefined && imagePath != null && imagePath != "") {
				imageData = imagePath.split("/");
				imageExtension = imagePath.split(".").pop();
				if(imageData.length > 5 && imageData[5] != undefined && imageData[5] != null && imageData[5] != "") {
					var renditionSize = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('#' + node +'-'+ imageData[5] + '').val();
					var $nodeName = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser');
					if(renditionSize != undefined && renditionSize != null && renditionSize != "" ) {                         
						var isFadeRequired = "";						
				       if(isFadeRequired = true  && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != undefined && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != null && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != "" ) {								
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').replaceWith('<div class="imagery is-gradient-bottom " style="background-image:url(&quot;'+destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 + '/jcr:content/renditions/rendition.'+ renditionSize +'.'+ imageExtension +'&quot;);">');					
						}else{
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 + '/jcr:content/renditions/rendition.'+ renditionSize +'.'+ imageExtension + ')');
						$("div.drop-block-offers-promo").addClass("drop-shaddow");
						}
					}
					else {
					var isFadeRequired = "";						
				       if(isFadeRequired = true  && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != undefined && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != null && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != "" ) {								
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').replaceWith('<div class="imagery is-gradient-bottom " style="background-image:linear-gradient(to right,'+ destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor+',transparent 100%), url(&quot;'+destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3  +'&quot;);">');					
						}else{
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 +')');
						$("div.drop-block-offers-promo").addClass("drop-shaddow");
						}
					}
				}
			}	
			//$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage + ')');
			$('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.drop-block-offers-title').append(destnRepoResult.destinationTitle);
		}
				
	}
	
</script> 
                  </div> 
                  <!-- drop-block end --> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>

                   <strong class="drop-block-title" tabindex="0">Latest fares</strong> 
                   <span class="forward drop-title"></span> 
                   <div> 
                    <!-- drop-block --> 
                    <!-- drop-block-offers --> 
                    <div class="drop-block-offers is-double"> 
                     <input type="hidden" id="horizontal-block-seletion" value="dynamicTeaser"> 
                     <div id="horizontal-block-horizontalDynamicTeaser"> 
                      <input type="hidden" id="horizontal-block-horizontal-3" value="205.153"> 
                      <input type="hidden" id="horizontal-block-origin" value="bom"> 
                      <input id="horizontal-block-destinationRepo" type="hidden" value="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/destinations/repository"> 
                      <div class="hidden horizontal-block-inputIataCodes">
                       CDG
                      </div> 
                      <div class="drop-block-offers-promo teaser-CDG"> 
                       <a target="_self"> 
                        <div class="imagery"></div> 
                        <div class="drop-block-offers-text"> 
                         <strong class="drop-block-offers-title"></strong> 
                         <span class="drop-block-offers-price"></span> 
                        </div> </a> 
                      </div> 
                      <div class="hidden horizontal-block-inputIataCodes">
                       JNB
                      </div> 
                      <div class="drop-block-offers-promo teaser-JNB"> 
                       <a target="_self"> 
                        <div class="imagery"></div> 
                        <div class="drop-block-offers-text"> 
                         <strong class="drop-block-offers-title"></strong> 
                         <span class="drop-block-offers-price"></span> 
                        </div> </a> 
                      </div> 
                     </div> 
                    </div> 
                    <!-- drop-block-more-link --> 
                    <div class="drop-block-more-link"> 
                     <a class="btn-more pull-right" href="/content/in/en/offers.html" target="_self">View more fares <span class="icon icon-arrow-right2 icon-rotate-rtl"></span> </a> 
                    </div> 
                    <script>
	$(document).ready(function() {
		try{
			var node = "horizontal-block";
			var seletion = $('#' + node + '-seletion').val();
			/*var origin = getCookieValue("fromIata");
			if (origin == undefined || origin == null || origin == '') {
				origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val();
			}*/
			var origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val();
			var pricingResponse = $getHPricingData(origin);
			var destinationIataCodes = $('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + node + '-inputIataCodes');
			if (seletion == 'dynamicTeaser') {
				$(destinationIataCodes).each(function() {
					var destination = $(this).text();

					var teaserNode = "teaser-" + destination;
					$getPricingDataHTeaser(node, teaserNode, pricingResponse, destination);
					$getDestinationRepoResultHTeaser(node, teaserNode, destination);
				});
			}
		} catch(err) {}
	});

	
	var $getPricingDataHTeaser = function(node, teaserNode, pricingResponse, destination) {
    	if(destination != undefined && destination != null && destination != "") {
            destination = destination.toUpperCase();
            destination = destination.trim();
        }
		
		 //console.log("pricingResponse::::::::::::" + pricingResponse);
		if(pricingResponse != undefined && pricingResponse != null && pricingResponse != "" && pricingResponse.length != 0) {
			var offerResponseArray = pricingResponse.offerResponseList;
			if (offerResponseArray.length != 0) {
				var currencyCode = offerResponseArray[0].currencyCode;
				var destinationFaresArray = offerResponseArray[0].destinationFares;
				if (destinationFaresArray.length != 0) {
					var destData = getDestinationPricingData(destinationFaresArray, destination);
					if (destData.length != 0) {
						$.each(destData[0].lowestFares, function(key, value) {
							if (value.cabinClass == 'ECONOMY') {
								$('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.drop-block-offers-price').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
								$('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('a').attr('href',value.deepLink);

							}
						});
					}
				}
			}
		}
				
	}

	var $getDestinationRepoResultHTeaser = function(node, teaserNode, destination) {
    	if(destination != undefined && destination != null && destination != "") {
            destination = destination.toUpperCase();
            destination = destination.trim();
        }
		var destinationRepoPath = $('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser').find('#' + node + '-destinationRepo').val();
		var destnRepoResult;
		getDestinationRepoData(destination,destinationRepoPath, function(data) {
			//console.log('getPricingResponse:' + data);
			destnRepoResult = data;
		});
		if (destnRepoResult != '' && destnRepoResult != undefined && destnRepoResult != null) {

			var imagePath = destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3;
			var imageData,imageExtension;
			if(imagePath != undefined && imagePath != null && imagePath != "") {
				imageData = imagePath.split("/");
				imageExtension = imagePath.split(".").pop();
				if(imageData.length > 5 && imageData[5] != undefined && imageData[5] != null && imageData[5] != "") {
					var renditionSize = $('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser').find('#' + node +'-'+ imageData[5] + '').val();
					var $nodeName = $('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser');
					if(renditionSize != undefined && renditionSize != null && renditionSize != "" ) {                         
						var isFadeRequired = "";
				       if(isFadeRequired = true  && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != undefined && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != null && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != "" ) {				
						
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').replaceWith('<div class="imagery is-gradient-bottom " style="background-image:linear-gradient(to right,'+ destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor+',transparent 100%), url(&quot;'+destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 + '/jcr:content/renditions/rendition.'+ renditionSize +'.'+ imageExtension +'&quot;);">');
					
						}else{
						
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 + '/jcr:content/renditions/rendition.'+ renditionSize +'.'+ imageExtension + ')');
						$("div.drop-block-offers-promo").addClass("drop-shaddow");
						}
					}else {
					var isFadeRequired = "";						
				       if(isFadeRequired = true  && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != undefined && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != null && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != "" ) {								
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').replaceWith('<div class="imagery is-gradient-bottom " style="background-image:linear-gradient(to right,'+ destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor+',transparent 100%), url(&quot;'+destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 +'&quot;);">');					
						}else{
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 +')');
						$("div.drop-block-offers-promo").addClass("drop-shaddow");
						}						
					}
				}
			}	
			$('#' + node + '-horizontalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.drop-block-offers-title').append(destnRepoResult.destinationTitle);
		}
				
	}
</script> 
                   </div>

                  <!-- drop-block --> 
                  <div class="drop-block pull-right"> 
                   <!-- drop-block-title -->
                   <strong class="drop-block-title" tabindex="0">Online services</strong> 
                   <span class="forward drop-title"></span> 
                   <!-- drop-block-offers --> 
                   <div></div> 
                   <input type="hidden" id="vertical-block33-seletion" value="staticTeaser"> 
                   <!-- drop-block-offers --> 
                   <div class="drop-block-offers"> 
                    <div class="drop-block-offers-promo"> 
                     <a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en-in/online-services.html" target="_self"> 
                      <div class="imagery" style="background-image: url(/content/dam/images/custom/mdd-offers-section-205x145/onlinemobile-services.png);"></div> 
                      <div class="drop-block-offers-text"> 
                       <strong class="drop-block-offers-title"> </strong> 
                       <span class="drop-block-offers-price">INR </span> 
                      </div> </a> 
                    </div> 
                   </div> 
                   <!-- drop-block-offers end --> 
                   <!-- drop-block-more-link --> 
                   <div class="drop-block-more-link"> 
                    <a class="btn-more pull-right" href=".html" target="_self">Learn more <span class="icon icon-arrow-right2 icon-rotate-rtl"></span> </a> 
                   </div> 
                   <!-- drop-block-more-link end --> 
                   <script>
	$(document).ready(function() {
		try{
			var node = "vertical-block33";
			var seletion = $('#' + node + '-seletion').val();
			/*var origin = getCookieValue("fromIata");
			if (origin == undefined || origin == null || origin == '') {
				origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val();
			}
			*/
			var origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val();
			var pricingResponse = $getHPricingData(origin);
			var destinationIataCodes = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + node + '-inputIataCodes');
			if (seletion == 'dynamicTeaser') {
				$(destinationIataCodes).each(function() {
					var destination = $(this).text();
					var teaserNode = "teaser-" + destination;
					$getPricingDataVTeaser(node, teaserNode, pricingResponse, destination);
					$getDestinationRepoResultVTeaser(node, teaserNode, destination);
				});
			}
		} catch(err) {} 
	});

	var $getHPricingData = function(origin) {
		var pricingResponse;
		if(origin != undefined && origin != null && origin != "") {
            origin = origin.toUpperCase();
            origin = origin.trim();
			getPricingResponse(origin, function(data) {
				//console.log('getPricingResponse:' + data);
				pricingResponse = data;
			});
		}
		return pricingResponse;
	}
	
	var $getPricingDataVTeaser = function(node, teaserNode, pricingResponse, destination) {

		if(destination != undefined && destination != null && destination != "") {
            destination = destination.toUpperCase();
            destination = destination.trim();
        }

		 //console.log("pricingResponse::::::::::::" + pricingResponse);
		if(pricingResponse != undefined && pricingResponse != null && pricingResponse != "" && pricingResponse.length != 0) {
			var offerResponseArray = pricingResponse.offerResponseList;
			if (offerResponseArray.length != 0) {
				var currencyCode = offerResponseArray[0].currencyCode;
				var destinationFaresArray = offerResponseArray[0].destinationFares;
				if (destinationFaresArray.length != 0) {
					var destData = getDestinationPricingData(destinationFaresArray, destination);
					if (destData.length != 0) {
						$.each(destData[0].lowestFares, function(key, value) {
							if (value.cabinClass == 'ECONOMY') {
								$('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.drop-block-offers-price').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
								$('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('a').attr('href',value.deepLink);

							}
						});
					}
				}
			}
		}
					
	}

	var $getDestinationRepoResultVTeaser = function(node, teaserNode, destination) {
		if(destination != undefined && destination != null && destination != "") {
            destination = destination.toUpperCase();
            destination = destination.trim();
        }
		var destinationRepoPath = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('#' + node + '-destinationRepo').val();
		var destnRepoResult;
		getDestinationRepoData(destination,destinationRepoPath, function(data) {
			//console.log('getPricingResponse:' + data);
			destnRepoResult = data;
		});
		if (destnRepoResult != '' && destnRepoResult != undefined && destnRepoResult != null) {
			var imagePath = destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3;
			var imageData,imageExtension;
			if(imagePath != undefined && imagePath != null && imagePath != "") {
				imageData = imagePath.split("/");
				imageExtension = imagePath.split(".").pop();
				if(imageData.length > 5 && imageData[5] != undefined && imageData[5] != null && imageData[5] != "") {
					var renditionSize = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('#' + node +'-'+ imageData[5] + '').val();
					var $nodeName = $('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser');
					if(renditionSize != undefined && renditionSize != null && renditionSize != "" ) {                         
						var isFadeRequired = "";						
				       if(isFadeRequired = true  && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != undefined && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != null && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != "" ) {								
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').replaceWith('<div class="imagery is-gradient-bottom " style="background-image:url(&quot;'+destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 + '/jcr:content/renditions/rendition.'+ renditionSize +'.'+ imageExtension +'&quot;);">');					
						}else{
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 + '/jcr:content/renditions/rendition.'+ renditionSize +'.'+ imageExtension + ')');
						$("div.drop-block-offers-promo").addClass("drop-shaddow");
						}
					}
					else {
					var isFadeRequired = "";						
				       if(isFadeRequired = true  && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != undefined && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != null && destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor != "" ) {								
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').replaceWith('<div class="imagery is-gradient-bottom " style="background-image:linear-gradient(to right,'+ destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3fadeColor+',transparent 100%), url(&quot;'+destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3  +'&quot;);">');					
						}else{
						$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage3 +')');
						$("div.drop-block-offers-promo").addClass("drop-shaddow");
						}
					}
				}
			}	
			//$nodeName.find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.imagery').css('background-image', 'url(' + destnRepoResult.mainHorizontalImage + ')');
			$('#' + node + '-verticalDynamicTeaser').find('.' + teaserNode + '').find('.drop-block-offers-title').append(destnRepoResult.destinationTitle);
		}
				
	}
	
</script> 
                  </div> 
                  <!-- drop-block end --> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div> 
              </div>

          <script>
		
function logout(){
$.ajax({
        url: "/bin/Logout",
		type: 'GET',   
		data: {"logOut":"logOut"},
        success: function(data) {           
            window.location.reload();
        },
         error:function(xhr,textStatus,errorThrown){
           window.location.reload();
	       console.log("logout failed!");
         }
    });
}
$('#profLogin,#profLogin2').click(function(){
	if( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
		window.open("https://m.qatarairways.com/mobile/deeplink/pagequery.htm?requestType=LOGIN&selLang=en", "_self");
    } 
    if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Mobile") != -1) {
		window.open("https://m.qatarairways.com/mobile/deeplink/pagequery.htm?requestType=LOGIN&selLang=en", "_self");
   }else{
		var cpmloginobj =$('#profLoginForm');
		$("#clbackurl1").val(document.URL);
		cpmloginobj.action = "https://cpm.qatarairways.com/cpm/views/verfiyUserQrHome.xhtml123?sellang=en";
		cpmloginobj.submit();
	}
});
</script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function() {
  var $C1headerImage = $('.C1-video-bg');
  var $mobileImageURL = $C1headerImage.data('mobile-image');
  var $desktopImageURL = $C1headerImage.data('desktop-image');
  var $mobileImageFadeColor = $C1headerImage.attr('data-mobile-fadeColor');
   var $desktopImageFadeColor = $C1headerImage.attr('data-desktop-fadeColor');
   var directionType = $('#fadeValue').val();
   var directionVal = (directionType == "qr.main") ? "to right" : "to left";

   if($mobileImageURL =='url();'){

   $mobileImageURL=$desktopImageURL;
   $mobileImageFadeColor =$desktopImageFadeColor;
   }
  $(function() {
         
		 if($(window).width() <= 750){
		   if($mobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $mobileImageFadeColor != ""){
		    $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$mobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$mobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		   }else{
		  	 $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$mobileImageURL);
             $("div.teaser-box-content").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		   }
           }else {
		    if($desktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $desktopImageFadeColor != ""){
		   $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$desktopImageFadeColor+',transparent 100%),'+$desktopImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		     }else{
		    $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$desktopImageURL);
            $("div.teaser-box-content").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		   }
            
         }
     });
 $(window).on('resize', function(){
   if($(this).width() <= 750){
     if($mobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $mobileImageFadeColor != ""){
			  $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$mobileImageFadeColor+',transparent 100%),'+$mobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		   }else{
		     $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$mobileImageURL);
             $("div.teaser-box-content").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		   }
   }else {
       if($desktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $desktopImageFadeColor != ""){
		   $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$desktopImageFadeColor+',transparent 100%),'+$desktopImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		     }else{
		    $C1headerImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$desktopImageURL);
            $("div.teaser-box-content").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		   }
         }
     });
	 
	 /* pricing code */
	 
	 var node = "video_image_copy";	
	 var dynamicIataCode = $('#' + node + '-dynamic').val();	
	 var origin = getCookieValue("fromIata");	 
	 var colorTheme = $('#' + node + '-colorText').val(); 
	  var buttonStyle = $('#' + node + '-buttonStyle').val(); 
		if (origin == undefined || origin == null || origin == '') {
			origin = $('#' + node + '-origin').val().toUpperCase().trim();			
		}
		
		$getVideoImagePricingData(colorTheme,buttonStyle,origin, dynamicIataCode);
		
});
var $getVideoImagePricingData = function(colorTheme, buttonStyle, origin, dynamicIataCode) {
if(dynamicIataCode != undefined && dynamicIataCode != null && dynamicIataCode != "") {
            dynamicIataCode = dynamicIataCode.toUpperCase().trim();	
           
        }
		var pricingResponse;
		getPricingResponse(origin, function(data) {				
			pricingResponse = data;
		});
		if(pricingResponse != undefined && pricingResponse != null && pricingResponse != "" && pricingResponse.length != 0) {
			var offerResponseArray = pricingResponse.offerResponseList;
			if (offerResponseArray.length != 0) {
				var currencyCode = offerResponseArray[0].currencyCode;
				var destinationFaresArray = offerResponseArray[0].destinationFares;
				if (destinationFaresArray.length != 0) {
					var destData = getDestinationPricingData(destinationFaresArray, dynamicIataCode);				
					if (destData.length != 0) {
						$.each(destData[0].lowestFares, function(key, value) {
							if (value.cabinClass == 'ECONOMY') {							
							if(colorTheme == 'white'){
									 switch(buttonStyle) {
									 case 'learnmore' :
									 $('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('strong').addClass('btn btn-white-transparent').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('a').attr({href: value.deepLink, target:'_blank'});
									 break;
									 
									 case 'purchase' :
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('strong').addClass('btn btn-orange').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('a').attr({href: value.deepLink, target:'_blank'});
									break;
									case 'nextstep' :
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('strong').addClass('btn btn-dark').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('a').attr({href: value.deepLink, target:'_blank'});
									break;
									 
									 }
									 
							
							}
							
							if(colorTheme == 'maroon'){
									switch(buttonStyle) {
									 case 'learnmore' :
									 $('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('strong').addClass('btn btn-dark-transparent').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
									 $('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('a').attr({href: value.deepLink, target:'_blank'});
									 break;
									 
									 case 'purchase' :
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('strong').addClass('btn btn-orange').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('a').attr({href: value.deepLink, target:'_blank'});
									break;
									case 'nextstep' :
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('strong').addClass('btn btn-dark').append(currencyCode + ' ' + value.lowestFare);
							$('.videoImage-dynamic-price').find('a').attr({href: value.deepLink, target:'_blank'});
									break;
									 
									 }
							}
							



							}
						});
					}
				}
			}
		}
}


</script>

         <script>
	var cuCurrentPagePath = $('#cuCurrentPagePath').val();
	$(document).ready(function() {
		var currentURL = window.location.pathname;
		//console.log('currentURL:' + currentURL);
		var tempSelector = currentURL.substring(currentURL.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
        //console.log('tempSelector:' + tempSelector);
		var elements = tempSelector.split('.');
        //console.log('elements:' + elements);
		var noOfElements = elements.length;
		//console.log('noOfElements::' + noOfElements);
		var selectedContactUsForm = '';
		if (noOfElements === 3) {
			selectedContactUsForm = elements[1];
			//console.log('selectedContactUsForm:' + selectedContactUsForm);
			$('#contactHelpTopicSelect').parent().find('.input-base-placeholder').addClass('visible');
			$('#contactHelpTopicSelect').parent().find('.custom-select-opener').css('padding','20px 30px 0 8px');
			$('#contactHelpTopicSelect').find('option').each(function() {
				var value = $(this).val();
				//console.log('value:' + value);
				var text = $(this).text();
				//console.log('text:' + text);
				var control = $(this).attr('data-control');
				if(selectedContactUsForm === value){
					$('#contactHelpTopicSelect').parent().find('.custom-select-opener').text($(this).text());
					return false;
				}
			});
		}

        $("#contactHelpTopicSelect").on('change', function() {		
            var value = $(this).val();
            //console.log('value:' + value);
            if(value !== 'default'){
                window.location =  cuCurrentPagePath + '.' + value + '.html';
            } else {
                window.location =  cuCurrentPagePath + '.html';
            }
        });

        $("#cufs .custom-select-dropdown ul.custom-select-list li").on('click', function() {		
            window.location =  cuCurrentPagePath + '.html';            
        });
	});


</script>

// Function added by vengadesh for campaigntracking cookie //
function trackingcookie(name,value,days) {
                                var exdate=new Date();
                                exdate.setTime(exdate.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
                                var values=escape(value) + ((days==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
                                document.cookie = name+"="+values+";domain=.qatarairways.com;path=/";
}
var strQueryString="";
var hasQueryStringURL = document.URL.indexOf('?');
var cookiName="";
var CookiValue="";
var tempCookiName="";
var cflag="";
if (hasQueryStringURL != -1)
  {
  strQueryString = document.URL.substring(hasQueryStringURL+1, document.URL.length);
  var firstParam=strQueryString.split('&');
  for(var i=0;i<firstParam.length;i++)
  {
  tempCookiName=firstParam[i].split("=");
  cookiName=tempCookiName.shift();
  cookiName=cookiName.toLowerCase()
  if(cookiName == "s_kwcid")
  {
   cflag="true";
   CookiValue=tempCookiName.pop();
  }
  if((cookiName =="cid") && (cflag == "" ))
  {
  CookiValue=tempCookiName.pop();
   }
                }
                if(CookiValue !=  "")
                {
                //alert(CookiValue);
                trackingcookie('campaigntracking',CookiValue,30);  
                }
}

function isArabic(strInput){
    var arregex = /[\u0600-\u06FF]/;
    if (arregex.test(strInput)){
                               return true;
    }else{
        return false;
      }
   }

$(window).on('load',function(){
     if($("#wcmmode").val() != 'editMode'){
// console.log('script calling on load');
 
   removeAllEmptyHeaderTags();
   removeAllEmptyHrefTags();
   removeAllEmptyPtags();

     }

});
   function removeAllEmptyHeaderTags(){

var allHeaderTags = document.querySelectorAll('h1,h2,h3,h4,h5,h6'),

    HeaderTags;


        for (var i = 0; i < allHeaderTags.length; i++) {
            HeaderTags = allHeaderTags[i];

            if (!HeaderTags.firstChild || HeaderTags.innerHTML == " ") {

                HeaderTags.parentNode.removeChild(HeaderTags);
            }
        }

   }

  

		
 function removeAllEmptyPtags(){
   var allParaTags = document.querySelectorAll('p');
    var ParaTags;
    for (var i = 0; i < allParaTags.length; i++) {
	   //ParaTags = allParaTags[i].textContent.trim();
       //allParaTags[i].innerHTML = ParaTags;
	   var allTags= allParaTags[i].getElementsByTagName('a');
	   
	   for (var j = 0; j < allTags.length; j++) {
          if( allTags[j].getAttribute("href") == "" ){
              allParaTags[i].removeChild(allTags[j]);
          }else if(allTags[j].innerHTML == ""){
		   allParaTags[i].removeChild(allTags[j]);
		  }
       }
     if (allParaTags[i].innerHTML == "")
     allParaTags[i].parentNode.removeChild(allParaTags[i]);
      }
     $('p').each(function() {
    var $this = $(this);
    if($this.html().replace(/\s|&nbsp;/g, '').length == 0)
        $this.remove();
});

  }


   function removeAllEmptyHrefTags(){
var anchorTags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
    for(var i = 0; i < anchorTags.length; i++) {
        if(anchorTags[i].getAttribute("href") == "" && anchorTags[i].textContent == "")
            anchorTags[i].parentNode.removeChild(anchorTags[i]);
    }
   }

</script>
